0                                   8717              * to use this prt, register r6 must be set to the desired
                                    8718              * return address if a line number is recognized
                                    8719              *
                                    8720              * R0 contains the specified line number on exit
                                    8721              * R1 has a delta that can be used by collect, move and copy
                                    8722              * R15 has return codes to show which way the line no was
                                    8723              * specified.
                                    8724              * R15 -  0 regular line number specified
                                    8725              *        4 first specified
                                    8726              *        8 current specified
                                    8727              *       12 last specified
                                    8728              *       16 end specified
                                    8729              *       20 next specified
                                    8730              *       24 previous specified
                                    8731              *       28 return specified
                                    8732              *       32 ATTN specified
                                    8733              *       36 ABORT specified
                                    8734              *
                                    8735              * after the line number specified has been processed,
                                    8736              * an increment is scanned for and added in if found
                                    8737              * unless cpfnoinc bit is on in cplflg4.
